# Icon Gallery

Below you can find a Table with all available icons in the library.
The table contains the name of the icon, its unicode value, and a preview of the icon itself.

```{tip}
You can look at the [Nerd Font Cheat Sheet](https://www.nerdfonts.com/cheat-sheet) for a list of all available icons.
Please note that the naming on the cheat sheet is not always the same as the naming in the library.
Use the unicode value to find the icon you are looking for in that case.
```

```{tip}
`Name`, `Unicode`, and `Unicode (Integer)` can be used to instantiate icons. 
Pleas have a look at the example gallery for more information on how to use the icons.
```
